padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1565541">ALakota</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-18">10/18/24 21:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It's not my style, but I respect it's quality and composition big time. Revisiting it now, I like it a fair deal more than I used to. I would definitely wear it over DHI or Original, but I don't feel old enough yet and I'm 38 lol. It seems to be a cultural thing, also. I think in the States, women don't expect this kind of scent and it seems a bit mature and ladies like something fresher or at least more "modern," but I've seen some over the top reactions to it in Europe. I don't want to be too general, because I'm sure to plenty of women in the US, this is the best men's fragrance they've ever smelled. If you like Dior Homme Intense or Dior Homme Original, of course you will most likely love this. Just be aware of what to expect, because it is a deeper, darker, more daring version of the Dior Homme iris-based lipstick-like DNA which to my nose is very mature, sophisticated, and classic-smelling, similar in its vibe to Prada L'Homme Intense and things like that roughly in it's character, not in its actual scent. They smell nothing alike really, but have a similar spirit. DHP has an incredibly deep scent character that develops over time like its predecessors, but is very satisfying throughout and consistent in its character. It's hard for me to rate just because it's not the sort of thing I love to wear, but I know for a fact that a ton of people do, So I give it high marks. Objectively speaking, it's a 10/10. I just wanted to warn people about its mature and heavy-duty scent character before someone goes blind-buying it for a fortune like it goes for here in the States, because the hype surrounding it is pretty hard to ignore. This is definitely not blind buy safe, and if it's hard to sample for you, try at least sampling Dior Homme Intense and see if you would see yourself wearing it, because it is unmistakably a deeper and bolder iteration of that scent to the point that many people without sensitive noses wouldn't be able to tell them apart in an obvious way. Again, if you like where Dior Homme Intense is going, this may be the final destination for you. Regardless of all that cautioning, if you're someone who has never experienced the Dior Homme line (Original Dior Homme, not the freshie 2020 versions, be warned of those differences also) then you should sample one of the three as soon as you can in order to familiarize yourself with the DNA, because it is unique and widely loved, and you may love it more than anything, as many do.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2320349"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2320349#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2318834" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2318834" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Smellybutgood"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1593587"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1593587.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="Smellybutgood" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.27417.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Dior Homme Parfum"title="Dior Homme Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2318834ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2318834" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1593587">Smellybutgood</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-17">10/17/24 11:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Before we get started, here are the notable Dior Homme iterations featuring iris over the years for your reference:<br />
<br />
●Dior Homme (2005) – The original iris masterpiece by Olivier Polge.<br />
●Dior Homme (2011) – Reformulated by François Demachy, retaining the iconic iris.<br />
●Dior Homme Intense (2011)<br />
●Dior Homme Parfum (2014) <br />
●Dior Homme Original (2021) – Re-release of the 2011<br />
<br />
In my opinion, and the opinions of many others', Dior Homme Parfum is the greatest fragrance release of all time. This is the only one I consistently buy whenever I'm notified it’s back in stock (since it’s been discontinued), I don’t hesitate—I grab a bottle. It’s just that special.<br />
<br />
What sets DHP apart from the others in the Dior Homme line, like DHI and DHOriginal, is its boldness. It takes the DNA of both and intensifies it, adding a depth and richness that the others can’t match. <br />
<br />
DHP works best in cooler weather, evenings, or any time you want to feel bold and sophisticated. While compliments are nice, I wear this fragrance for myself—it's about how I feel when I wear it.<br />
<br />
Some love its daring, bold nature, while others might find it too intense. But that’s exactly what makes it unique. It’s not for everyone—and that’s why I love it. For introverts like me, DHP lets the fragrance speak for you. Its sophistication and depth are undeniable.<br />
<br />
An absolute masterpiece. If you can get your hands on a bottle and prefer a bold, refined scent, don’t hesitate—you won’t regret it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2318834"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2318834#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2280215">divineintervation1994</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-08">10/08/24 11:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Beastmode performance, manlier and sexier than the dior homme intense with less lipstick vibes thanks to the added leather note. Opening is a bit too sour for me but it turns out to be a masterpiece of a fragrance. Yes, it costs more but go with this one rather than Intense. More wearable even though it is stronger.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2308984"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2308984#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2307803" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1995085">JaySentz</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-29">09/29/24 10:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This was not love at first sniff, just a heavy lipstick iris and warm amber dry down. Smells like a leathery makeup bag, why do people like this so much?….<br />
<br />
It took a few real wears and after having this gently swirling around me for a few days I get it. The leather rose is not really noticeable until the iris fades a bit and then this lingers as nice ambery vanilla. It’s comforting and sophisticated at the same time.  I was hoping for a more noticeable leather and oud (faint at best) to balance the sweet iris but the gentle touches make it more nuanced and if you don’t like leather or oud there probably isn’t enough to put you off. Rose isn’t prominent either. Performance is amazing too, one spray radiated off my wrist for hours!<br />
<br />
This is pretty addictive and I wouldn’t change anything, but if I feel like a little more edge it layers well with a leather scent like Guilty Absolute. One of the best designer fragrance of all time seemed a stretch, now I can’t really disagree.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2299068"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2299068#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2299004" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2270682" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TWN2RBO"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1946489"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1946489.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TWN2RBO" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Kerosene/Blackmail-47483.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.47483.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Blackmail"title="Blackmail"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2270682ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2270682" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1946489">TWN2RBO</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-03">09/03/24 19:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The best smelling fragrance is subjective, I never understood why a grown person bashes someone’s opinion on such a topic. One thing is for certain, my nose has changed throughout my fragrance collecting days and I use to hate DHI for its lip stick vibe. Perhaps it’s the macho man inside of me. For this reason, I closed my mind off to DHP for years bc I think most flankers smell the same and it’s a corporate cash grab..until someone sent me a sample of DHP last year. <br />
I just sprayed it on my hand before jumping into bed to write this. The deep facets of leather and iris make something very cozy and creamy. This is the perfect amount of sweetness, nothing gourmand to me, perfectly woodsy, it’s cozy, comforting, sexy, dark, and mysterious all at once. <br />
99% of my collection is niche at this point of my life, DHP and 9 Tom Fords make up my designer shelf, love them all, but this is a powerhouse, and I love it. If you didn’t like DHI and found it too feminine or lip stickish, I highly recommend you try this. The leather note in DHP gave it just the right amount of gentleman status and DHI should have been this way since they market it towards men and don’t sell DHP in the states anymore. <br />
9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2270682"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2270682#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2267545" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2267545" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="DSK"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1013737"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1013737.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="DSK" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Bvlgari/Aqva-Pour-Homme-Marine-1742.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.1742.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Aqva Pour Homme Marine"title="Aqva Pour Homme Marine"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2267545ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2267545" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1013737">DSK</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-31">08/31/24 18:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I own a 2018 version of this fragrance (75 ml). I can report exactly what @local7 said a couple of comments below. I sprayed heavily a 2024 version in a duty free shop and it definitely has a different opening than my version. It actually reminded me of how this fragrance smelled when it was released in 2014. Like a very concentrated version of Dior Homme Intense. WIth a smooth delicious cocoa and leather and less prominant rose. I was intially blown away by this and just as I was considering splasing to get the new bottle as well (although my 75ml bottle is almost full) the fragrance started to settle down very much became almost identical to the one I have. I do not like how rose became a very prominant note in this fragrance over the years. I think back when it was released it was a much smoother creamy buttery cocoa mixed with leather and the new version reminded me of this with its opening. I repeat the in the drydown though they smell more or less the same as other recent versions of this fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2267545"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2267545#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2265467" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2265467" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Xhpeyulhp"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2019046"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2019046.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Xhpeyulhp" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Serge-Lutens/Ambre-Sultan-2760.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.2760.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Ambre Sultan"title="Ambre Sultan"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2265467ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2265467" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2019046">Xhpeyulhp</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-30">08/30/24 00:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Absolutely stunning masterpiece. Definitely the most luscious of the whole family of Dior Hommes, beautifully complex and multi-faceted. On my skin, the concentration is strong, maybe too strong in the opening, which is thick with rose and oud and fruit and leather. But after an hour or so, everything begins to calm down and all the beautiful layers start to reveal themselves more clearly. It's like Dior went on vacation to the UAE to visit his rose-oud-drenched buddies and he enthusiastically embraced it all, wearing a ghutra, learning Arabic, drinking 'ahweh instead of café... But then after a while he came back to himself, remembered how beautiful his native French culture was and integrated the best of both worlds. I love this juice—the opening makes it a bit challenging for me to wear at first, but the luscious drydown is more than worth it. I've fallen in love all its wondrous levels of awesomeness, and I want to hang on to it forever, it's so beautiful.<br />
<br />
I should say that I appreciate everything in this line. I think of the various Dior Homme releases like this: if Cologne is the gin and tonic on a hot summer day, then Dior Homme (2020) is like a sparkling rosé; Sport is like sangria; Eau for Man is the beaujolais; OG is the burgundy; Intense is the bordeaux; and Parfum is that exquisite Hermitage La Chapelle that needs an hour in the decanter to open up properly before you can really taste it. It's not that one release is better than another; instead, they each stand on their own, in different situations and contexts. Sometimes, you want a g&amp;t with your hors-d'œuvres; but sometimes you're serving up roast chicken—or pâté and saucisson sec, or ratatouille, or dauphinoise potatoes, or rack of lamb—and something else will be much better suited. And you don't have to give up wine with dinner just because you had a cocktail beforehand, or forgo a good martini before supper starts just because you know a good Côtes-du-Rhône is gonna be on the table. <br />
<br />
So back to this Parfum, which is my Hermitage. I would like to die smelling like this. ❤️</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2265467"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2265467#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2260189" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2260189" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="local7"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1547197"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1547197.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="local7" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2260189ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2260189" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1547197">local7</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-25">08/25/24 00:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I guess it depends on what the definition of reformulated is but I got a bottle with batch code 4F01 (June of this year) and it's without a doubt different from my 2022 and 2023 bottles. My daughter went to Paris with friends and they picked me up this bottle from the Dior Boutique on 30 Avenue Montaigne. I let them smell one of my bottles before they left and they thought it was very good. They tried it in the store when they bought my bottle and the first thing they said when they got back was "hey try this, it's different from yours - we even told the lady at the counter about the one you let us try and she said maybe yours had just aged over time."<br />
<br />
So I tried it. It's different. HOWEVER, it's not (1) weaker OR (2) worse. From what I can tell, the rose and sandalwood are not as prominent and the leather note comes out much faster and is stronger. It's still very beautiful and I actually may like it more than the others. This one seems a tiny bit tamer but it's still very strong and honestly the older ones are almost too strong. So it could be batch variation with where they sourced the rose  or other naturals (in the Nose documentary it was communicated that Demachy had very specific suppliers, for instance the rose growers in France who have both a passion for their roses and exacting standards).<br />
<br />
I'm no expert, but since three other people who are not at all involved in fragrance first noticed it themselves and then I also noticed, there does seem to be evidence of a difference BUT NOT necessarily for the worse, by any means. NOBODY in the group considerd it worse or inferior. Just different. I do not in any way think this has been cheapened.<br />
<br />
So take it for what it's worth. There seems to be some change but not bad change. The other three thought the new was "more fruitier" where the old was more heavy on sandalwood, more woody. I think the leather note is still the prominent note in both and they are all great. So even if there is some change, it absolutely lives up to the name.<br />
<br />
Edit:<br />
<br />
It's the next day. For the sake of fairness I sprayed one spray of each on each hand. On the immediate spray there is maybe a slight hint of more orange or rose on the older but after 2 minutes they are, to me, identical. So maybe it's just their first impression, maybe it's a slight difference in how much musk or something that makes the initial spray slightly different but within minutes they actually seem the same. If you smell the dispensers, the old smacks your nose harder with the leather note. That's the only difference I can tell for sure. But ultimately spraying on skin, they are same to me. The new is still undeniably awesome. I'm not concerned and happy that I now have three bottles. Will keep racking them up every chance I get.<br />
<br />
My 23 year old daughter jut arrived. It's been 15 m since I sprayed. She smelled each hand. This is her assessment: there is definitely a difference - the older is stronger, the newer is weaker. The older is more "gritty" and the newer is "smoother" and more subtle. I'm just reporting. My nose is 30 years older but there's the data. Again to me, I can't tell a difference. She can.<br />
<br />
One hour and a half later: According to daughter, the new is STRONGER than the old so far in dry down.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2260189"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2260189#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2258864" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1915840">c0ca1nel0ve</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-15">08/15/24 21:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>GOD, THIS IS PERFECTION!!! One of my favorites in the collection, one of my favorites PERIOD, this is such a beautiful composition by the genius François Demachy! I'm in ought every time i spray this, whether it's on my hand or experiencing the sillage, this is what i would call a masterpiece, it's such delicate powdery iris and woods and leather! but enough fanboying over DHP i'll try to explain it the best i can, in the opening i get very very little orange it's hardly noticeable u have to really dig ur nose in it to smell the orange, i get mostly a big blast of beautiful iris that is more waxy than powdery in the opening, as it dries down the cedar start getting more obvious and the leather starts popping up but all these facets are complimentary to the iris, they all sort of give u different angles of the iris, the cedar sometimes gives a sharp feel, sometimes the leather gives it a velvety complimentary touch but ultimately my favorite part of this composition is how beautifully the iris and the sandalwood works together, it's like a heavenly powdery velvety experience complimented by the leather and cedar and ofc not to forget the gorgeous ambrette which gives it a fluffy musky feel, overall i think this is beautifully done by François Demachy i think every part of this composition goes brilliantly together, but some notes here doesn't really come to my nose all that much, like the rose and the oud, i get the oudy facet more than the rose i get very little rose, and what i'd call an illusion of oud not a full bodied oud more like a base of which everything else is built on, to sum it all up, gorgeous lovely waxy powdery elegant masterpiece i always love every minute of wearing it, and as a plus this fragrance lasts and projects like no other, even the newer formulation i have lasts until the next day and projects for 3-4 hours massively,</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Are they wrong? Meh.<br />
It definitely has a lipsticky tint, but it works. I find that the leather and iris combination dominate for a very long time, as I can barely smell the oud, cedar and rose in it eight hours later, while the iris-leather still blasts me. I don't mind it, though.<br />
<br />
If you like the old Iris Dior Homme's, this one turns it even more chocolate-y and dark.<br />
9.5/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2235400"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2235400#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2231562" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1260156">MrMrOverHere</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-16">07/16/24 18:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'm an evangelist for not buying something until you've sampled it, but today I came SO CLOSE to blind buying this because I saw it for a decent price and everyone seems so up in arms about how great this thing is and how difficult it is to come by. Didn't do it, though, because I had a vague memory of having sampled it a couple of years ago, so I pulled out the big orange leather suitcase where I keep all my old sample vials and after about half an hour of sifting through them, I finally laid hands on it. There were only a couple sprays left, but they were enough to remind me of what I subconsciously had remembered all along: I don't care for this. I can tell it's good, but the vibe that this fragrance portrays isn't something I ever feel like on a day-to-day basis. I feel like I don't own enough neckties to wear it regularly. But like I said, this is objectively great-- I totally see why people like it. I'm just not one of those people. Plus I've got a couple other irisy leathers (1996 and Soleil de Jeddah) that already scratch this basic itch for me. <br />
<br />
So with this fragrance more than most fragrances, I think it's really important to sample before buying because there's so much pressure to scoop it up "before it's gone for good," and that might influence some people to act rashly and end up with buyer's remorse. I've seen reviewers who never encourage blind buying do a 180 on this one and be like, "this is the exception-- blind buying is encouraged in this case." And I'm all for people having an opinion, but that's just shitty advice. Sample it first, then seek it out if it's your fave. Just don't buy into the hype until you've formed your own opinion.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2220662"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2220662#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2220408" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2212989"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2212989#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2211288" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2211288" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Jaype"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1833624"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1833624.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Jaype" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Amouage/Figment-Man-45292.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.45292.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Figment Man"title="Figment Man"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2211288ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2211288" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1833624">Jaype</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-07">07/07/24 16:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I put this one off for the longest time as it was heavily hyped. But, out of the whole line, I prefer DHP, as I don't enjoy smelling like a lipstick, which Intense definitely does. This is more amber/woody niche, much more my vibe.<br />
<br />
I would advise restraint in spraying. One must ensure you want this on you for the long haul (&gt;10 hrs), as once sprayed, this will not scrub off easily. <br />
<br />
If you can't bear powdery fragrances, go elsewhere. This is extremely powder-heavy. Well, enough with the warnings.<br />
<br />
Dior Homme Parfum is a powerful, dense, long-lasting juice, with huge projection. It is extremely smooth after the whack of its opening fades.<br />
<br />
The iris in the opening is loud and it lingers throughout. I detect the orange in the opening, but once that fades you are in for more iris, rich creamy oris butter and varnished dark wood. <br />
<br />
After an hour or two the heart/middle evolves to an oppulence of jammy rose with almost dark chocolate hints. The varnished wood remains and the leather starts to be more prevalent.<br />
<br />
Balsamic but creamy in the drydown with the ambrette musk. I'm not sure there's real oud in here.<br />
<br />
I imagine this fragrance might be a bit much for some, especially if you have a weak stomach or are a bit under the weather. It's the type of scent that could be potentially unbearable.<br />
<br />
For particular evenings, cooler weather and dressing up, this could be a perfect scent. But I can't easily imagine it working well dressed down or for a casual meetup.<br />
<br />
I see this working on +35-year-old guys (maybe an ageing rocker) or very confident dark, steamy women. It's the type of fragrance that demands something of the wearer.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2211288"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2211288#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2209854" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

It smells very natural and yet sophisticated. You use some colognes for the general admiration of other people. But Dior homme parfum is much more than that. <br />
Reading the gentleman’s review below made me realize what a great and beautiful perfume Dior Homme Parfum is. <br />
<br />
I must start to say; I did wear Dior Homme Intense yesterday for the first time also and I was swept away by the cent and performance. <br />
<br />
I knew Parfum would need to step up the plate to beat Intense from yesterday’s performance. <br />
<br />
The DHI after 10 hours I could still have a soft cent bubble around me. <br />
<br />
The DHP after 8 hours the cent bubble was dying out and by 10 hours it was pure skin cent. <br />
<br />
But, the Intense does smell like a cent for the masses to enjoy where the Parfum is more for the older more masculine type that are sophisticated. <br />
<br />
The orange and Iris in the opening is a bit overpowering but the powdery note does make it acceptable for the beginning. <br />
<br />
The orange note soon fades away and the leather and musk with powder comes out for a while. <br />
<br />
For me, to my surprise the cent comes back, almost as stage 3 with the musk and the woody notes very smoothly dying out to the final skin cent alone. <br />
<br />
This is an amazing fragrance and I would give mine 10/10 <br />
<br />
Performance and cent is top level.<br />
<br />
Had 3 compliments today which never really happens. <br />
<br />
DHP - I LOVE YA… very satisfied much.<br />
<br />
  “Someone, give that perfumer a Bells!”</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2180231"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2180231#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2179484" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1441264">davidramos555</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-05">06/05/24 20:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Let me start off by saying I am absolutely in love with Dior Homme Intense. That being said, I recently took the plunge and ordered the Parfum version. It just came in today and upon first sniff of this I have fallen in love all over again in an even deeper way with this new buy of mine, Dior Homme Parfum. <br />
<br />
Dior Homme Intense would be falling in love with your high school sweet heart.<br />
<br />
Dior Homme Parfum would be reuniting with your long lost high school sweetheart 20 years later when you’re all grown up and have much more to offer and have settled in life. <br />
<br />
Scent: Very simply put, is, Dior Homme Intense DNA with a slight orangey vibe in the background upon initial spray, the chocolate vibes are elevated as well, much stronger in the Parfum version.<br />
<br />
After about 20-30 min the initial spray elevates with the most beautiful soft rose and soft leather. Neither are overpowering but they add such depth to this cologne, it really does take Dior Homme Intense to the next level.<br />
<br />
Absolute beautiful Perfumery here!!! Genius almost!! I loved it so much upon the first spray today I just purchased a second bottle. I never want this one to run out. Definitely back up bottle worthy.<br />
<br />
Longevity: I sprayed it at 1pm today and it’s 1030pm now and I can still smell this in the air. An absolute powerhouse. <br />
<br />
Guys run and get this. It is hard to come by and very expensive but if you can afford it get it, run don’t walk. Consider a back up bottle as I have, you won’t regret it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2179484"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2179484#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2174524" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This perfume could be perfect for me if the rose and the leather note would be replaced by something more interesting. Unfortunately on my skin the rose and the leather are the most prominent. Other then that nice comforting perfume.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2174524"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2174524#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2172848" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2172848" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Smellybutgood"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1593587"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1593587.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="Smellybutgood" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.27417.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Dior Homme Parfum"title="Dior Homme Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2172848ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2172848" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1593587">Smellybutgood</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-30">05/30/24 17:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Dior stunned the world with Dior Homme in 2005. <br />
<br />
Just two years later, in 2007, they amazed fragrance enthusiasts again with Dior Homme Intense. <br />
<br />
In 2014, they outdid themselves with Dior Homme Parfum, a scent many consider one of the best designer fragrances ever created. I mean, this stuff would give any niche fragrance a serious run.<br />
<br />
This legendary fragrance opens with a captivating blend of seductive iris and robust masculine leather. Its a unique fragrance with an original scent and strong performance that is perfect for dates, intimate encounters, and formal events.<br />
<br />
However, this fragrance is not easy to wear. It is challenging, sharp, mature, oud/iris-centric, and loud—BUT it smells incredible.<br />
<br />
Dior is my favorite fragrance house and Dior Homme Parfum is among my top 3 favorite offerings from the house.<br />
<br />
Unfortunately it has been discontinued so get it while you can.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2172848"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2172848#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2171160" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2171160" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="hugo1dk"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1868615"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1868615.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="hugo1dk" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Xerjoff/Symphonium-59707.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.59707.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Symphonium"title="Symphonium"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2171160ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2171160" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1868615">hugo1dk</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-29">05/29/24 04:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The best designer fragrance ever perfumed.<br />
<br />
This fragrance is not what i expected, but in a very good way. This is quite far from the modern Dior Homme Intense, it doesn't have that intense, synthetic extremely powdery iris that intense dose. This tones the powder down alot, it smells much less like makeup, thank goodness. My first spray of this threw me off, i expected a powdery makeup but with a darker wood and leather and that added rose. But no, this was, almost fresh? but WOW, this is incredible. An absolutely gorgeous scent. My grandmother, mother and father absolutely loved this scent and kept coming back to be to ask to smell the test strip again and again.<br />
<br />
One word to describe it,<br />
ELEGANT<br />
<br />
This stuff is beyond rich, dense, complex, addicting and intriguing. Emphasis on rich. It keeps one captivated for AGES and leaves a scent in your nose and in impression on your brain wanting you to smell it again.<br />
<br />
I would go on about technicalities regarding this fragrance, but all one needs to know is this is HEAVENLY. One of if not the designer fragrance i will reach for time and time again. <br />
<br />
Performance: 10/10 15+hours<br />
Projection: 8/10 <br />
Smell; 10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2171160"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2171160#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2166529" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2166529" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="timmybils"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1773009"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1773009.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="timmybils" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/SpongeBob-Squarepants/Squidward-28290.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.28290.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Squidward"title="Squidward"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2166529ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2166529" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1773009">timmybils</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-24">05/24/24 09:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If you are reading the reviews trying to compare Dior Homme Parfum with Dior Homme Intense without getting some testers, let me help you to decide since I got them both;<br />
<br />
TLDR: Side by side, the DHI is more floral, bright, airy, powdery, lipstick unisex frag, while DHP is a rich, dark, creamy, woody, subtly sweet frag. <br />
I prefer this DHP. The dry down smells almost exactly like Amouage Enclave.<br />
<br />
First, I got DHI and didn't really like it. I saw the rave reviews on it and I was absolutely not understanding the hype. It smelled like someone shot a bottle of powder in my face, that mixed with the smell of lipstick I was disgusted. Instead of giving it away, I thought I'll hold onto it and let it steep over time with the air in it that was introduced when I sprayed it.<br />
....9 months later, after spraying it less and not in front of me and actually being told by several women that I smelled really good without any prompts. I started dating this guy who liked spraying it (2-3 sprays) on himself and I slowly came around to it. When I first got it it was in the late spring, early summer and it was mid 70's outside. The aforementioned guy was spraying it on during the winter and at night.<br />
<br />
I got the Dior Homme Parfum this week and let me tell you, this one is waaaay better. Adding the orange in the opening, the subtle leather tones and the bit of oud has transformed the iris from a lipsticky (Iris is a prominent ingredient in lipstick) makeup bag, powder mess into a dark, rich, masculine forward statement. <br />
<br />
Side by side, the DHI is more floral, bright, airy, powdery, lipstick unisex frag, while DHP is a rich, dark, creamy, woody, subtly sweet frag. Both of them project amazingly, and are 10+ hours, 24hours+ on clothes. If you wear them in the summer, never above 78F or in the daytime, or when doing physical activities where you are sweating. Spray no more than 3 sprays each elbow and 1 on the back of the neck. <br />
<br />
DO NOT SPRAY DHP or DHI ON YOUR CHEST OR FRONT NECK. This projects way too much. This is a sillage monster and does not go away.<br />
<br />
At discounters DHI 150ml 150.USD. DHP 100ml 170.USD</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2166529"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2166529#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2161674" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; ConUS.<br />

I don't like the vast majority of designer fragrances, but this really is exceptional.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2161674"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2161674#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2159698" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I've never wanted to gatekeep a fragrance so bad, but as a lover of this community I have to spread the love of this amazing fragrance. From start to finish Dior Homme Parfum has Absolutely shocked me in terms of how powerful and strong this fragrance really is. When I say this stuff can last over 12 hours.... I am not joking. The fragrance starts off with a very strong and powdery iris note that I feel like it may take some getting used to if your nose is sensitive. Over time this fragrance begins to dry down into a leatherier masterpiece. This fragrance gives you no choice but to stand up with your chest pointed out making sure that you exude as much confidence as humanly possible. It's sweet but not in a very feminine way, which is crazy considering the slight floral Rosey note that appears during the middle dry down of this fragrance. If you are not a fan of the fragrance that sticks around like crazy and projects like crazy, then this is not the Frangrance for you. In conclusion, I would like to rate this fragrance a solid 9.4/10 ( I am very strict with my ratings) Thank you for reading my review!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I am starting to get into more challenging niche perfumery and have only scratched the surface, but this can definetely be a niche scent. This is deep, rich, powdery, creamy, and woody. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2133600" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ayywolf"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1946008"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1946008.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ayywolf" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2133600ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2133600" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1946008">ayywolf</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-23">04/23/24 06:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Upon the initial spary, I get DHI but the rose and leather really starts coming through right away. This is a very floral scent, much more floral than I had thought. It's also much sweeter than what I expected, leaving me with a drydown that is very similar to Valentino Uomo Intense but much more medicinal and syrupy. To be honest, I wanted to like this fragrance but the floral touch is too much for me personally. Interestingly enough, this would make a very memorable feminine fragrance and I think many women use it. It's extremely heavy in a good way, very sophisticated and dense, insane performance on this one.<br />
For me, I would use DHI if I want the effect that I expected this fragrance to bring. This is not as powdery as the rest of the Dior Homme line, but if I was famous and went to an award show, this would 100% be the scent I'd apply. If you love iris scents, this might be a letdown, as I feel DHI has more of an iris-heavy smell, while this one only lets the iris shine in the opening in my experience. If I want something of this DNA, I would honestly go for Valentino Uomo Intense, because that one doesn't remind me of cough syrup as much as this one on the drydown.<br />
Insane performance but I'm not buying a full bottle for a long time.<br />
7/10 for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2133600"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2133600#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2133296" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
I wouldn’t say it’s my most worn as it feels you need to be dressed accordingly but I find myself just having a spray at home often because I love the scent so much. <br />

<br />
1. Dior Homme Original [2021] (fresh yet sweet, round, clean iris— simple perfection)<br />
2. Dior Homme Intense (almost vanillicish-pearish-round smell, nice but sort of generic and overpowering the iris, the most "feminine" of the three)<br />
3. Dior Homme Parfum (biting cough syrup component, the leather isn't a great quality leather so maybe that's the issue, too much clouding the iris, clunky)<br />
<br />
Dior Homme Original is the "weakest" of the three, but I'd rather re-spray and smell amazing than smell like the others more intensely/for longer. Fresh fragrances are almost always going to be less in your face, but I'm okay with embracing their fleeting nature, especially when they're as beautiful as Dior Homme Original.<br />
<br />
I get that the parfum is the most sought after by far, so I guess I'm in the minority here!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2114640"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2114640#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2111454" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Just working with similar notes.<br />
It was a bottom layer of L’Eau d’Issey Pour Homme Or Encens, mid layer of The One Mysterious Nights, and a top layer of Dior Homme Parfum. <br />
<br />
All have rose and two of them have either labdanum, leather, sandalwood, oud, cedar and amber. Those notes amped up with their differences makes this one of the most amazing scents everyone should try if they have it. It's a powerhouse with monster projection and will last you throughout the day with just one spray of each. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1896091">Glue</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-27">03/27/24 10:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This was sort of a blind buy for me. Sampled the Intense version from a friend and I liked it so I assumed I will like this one even more based on the notes breakdown. <br />
The opening is a bit boring to me, you can mainly smell the lipstick and leather. A bit disappointing, Gentleman Eau de Parfum Reserve Privée has much better opening than this one. This one really shines in the drydown when the iris and leather tone down and you start smelling the lovely rose notes. <br />
The performance is pretty good, I was expecting more based on the reviews but still ok. Sillage and projection are not very strong on my skin, I'd say moderate. But it does stay on my skin for a long time, it's been over 6 hours since I sprayed it and I still smell it just sitting at my desk.<br />
Probably more suitable choice for formal occasions, evenings and dates but honestly I'll just wear it whenever I want to smell nice.<br />
Not a safe buy, sample first. I do like it but it's not a love at first sniff.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2105922"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2105922#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2104388" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
If you own DHI and feel you might not need this please do all you can to at least sample this, it's a level above.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2087203"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2087203#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2086749" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2086749" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="BalkanFragranceLover"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1212098"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1212098.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="BalkanFragranceLover" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Boucheron/Feve-Tonka-de-Canaima-72360.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.72360.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Fève Tonka de Canaima"title="Fève Tonka de Canaima"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2086749ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2086749" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1212098">BalkanFragranceLover</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-08">03/08/24 22:43</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Got a bottle of the newest formulation that comes in a 100mL bottle.<br />
2-3 days of wearing and comparing it to my 2017 DHI.<br />
Side by side with DHI, Parfum is a less loud in the opening, the sweetness is toned down and it comes of more as a floral and woody, rather than sweet powdery like DHI.<br />
On the drydown, Parfum leans significantly on the rose accord, and the Iris note is a lot less prominent. <br />
While there is a hint of it, DHP is not a heavy leather fragrance at all, and the rose is much more prominent than leather or woods. <br />
As far as performance goes - it depends on what a person is accustomed to i guess. People accustomed to middle-eastern style perfumery will be thoroughly unimpressed with what DHP has to offer in projection and staying power, but this is French perfumery, and is traditionally not as loud and pungent as the middle eastern ones. <br />
So the "beast mode" hype this fragrance usually gets, will be a bit misleading to people who wear Amouage Interlude or something similar. It is not nearly in the same category. For a designer scent from a french house - more than ok, but still, not even close to Sauvage Elixir for example, which i would say is closer to middle eastern type than a classic French perfumery. <br />
Is it redundant to own both DHP and DHI? <br />
Well, not completely. DHI is louder, sweeter and brighter, and a lot more linear than DHP, which in turn is more toned down on the opening, and a bit more sophisticated on the drydown. But the differences are subtle, and the scent profiles are still, very similar, you could interchange between them on any occasion without second thoughts.<br />
So my conclusion is, if you absolutely love the original style of the Dior Homme line, and money are not an issue (DHP is VERY rare online, and costs like 180 euro for the 100mL) yeah, absolutely get it.<br />
If you have set budget and already own DHI, you can safely pass on DHP - it is too similar (while still having differences) and for that price i would say, go for your preferred niche house - you will get more from it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2086749"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2086749#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2085362" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
