padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2083769" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Opato"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1828390"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1828390.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Opato" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2083769ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2083769" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1828390">Opato</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-06">03/06/24 02:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The impression from the opening notes is a perfect blend of leather and an incredible subtile, yet stout, freshness that perfectly evokes the authoritative expression that a lot of reviewers mention below. <br />
In the mid, the oud-ish notes comes forward and mingles with whiffs of rose, iris and talcum. Eventually the leather subsides and the drydown settles with contrasting notes from the mid, with wood and a deeper oud impression. <br />
<br />
I consider this an incredibly pleasant scent with very interesting contrasts that makes me curious. Yet it is not a bottle I would not seek out myself, since the talcum and oud combination is a too strong reminiscence with the lovely Arabic lady who ran the local grocery store where I lived ca. 1993. So for me, the opening impression morphs into a too feminine dry down.<br />
<br />
Talcum is a note I personally avoid in perfumery. It is what most people for some reason refer to as "powdery", even if the powder they refer to is not necessarily composed of talcum. I do not necessarily associate talcum with women's purses – there are also memories of rock climbing or the backstage of theatre – but it is a bit misplaced in perfumes I think. I am used to it being something that is to be showered off after work/leisure or something that women whish to mask with more top heavy feminine perfumes. But that does not change the fact that I love to smell Dior Homme Parfum from time to time.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2083769"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2083769#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2081590" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2080537" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RandolphCanuck"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/73594"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.73594.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="RandolphCanuck" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Neroli-Portofino-12192.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.12192.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Neroli Portofino"title="Neroli Portofino"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2080537ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2080537" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/73594">RandolphCanuck</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-02">03/02/24 22:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After extensive side-by-side testing, I conclude that current Dior Homme Parfum is every bit as good and as the original 75 ml version.  Like many here have expressed, I was initially disappointed with my new bottle, acquired late last summer at Charles de Gaulle Airport duty free.  It did not perform well right out of the box, seeming weak and somewhat one-note.  So after several frustrating wearings, I decided to put it away for a while.  <br />
<br />
Six months later, and there's been a transformation!  What I now have is as potent and complex as the vintage.  And it smells virtually identical, from initial spray to late dry down.  I won't elaborate on how special this fragrance is, as that's been well documented already.  I would just urge a little patience.  The new bottles need some air in them and a few months to maturate.  That's all.  My batch codes are 4W02 and 3F02 for my 2014 and 2023 bottles, respectively.  And yes, the formulation code on both boxes is the same, 08642/A.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2080537"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2080537#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2077669" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2076500"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2076500#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2076482" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2076482" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="youripufje"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2036418"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2036418.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="youripufje" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2076482ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2076482" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2036418">youripufje</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-28">02/28/24 02:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After going through a bottle of the original formulation of DHI and halfway through my 'new' 150ML bottle of DHI I finally ventured to a sample of Dior Homme Parfum. In short, I'm baffled by the upgrade in quality, smoothness and blend of this compared to the DHI I am so familiar with. <br />
<br />
As other have commented, Parfum's opening is immediately addictive and allures you to drench every inch of your body in it - if it wasn't for the suffocating thickness and syrupiness of the scent bubble. <br />
<br />
Parfum is an extremely iconic blend that I can not get enough of after 2 days of wearing. It's very unfortunate the performance does not seem that impressive on my skin. Similar to my recent bottle of DHI I suppose. <br />
<br />
Even after years of subscribing to this hobby my nose is not developed enough to pick out individual notes so I can only describe it as a clear make-up, floral, deep scent that makes me think of a high-end leather designer purse carrying lipstick and sanitary products. <br />
<br />
Contrary to others I don't find this hard to wear at all, but then again I am not one to believe certain fragrances can only be worn in certain circumstances.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2076482"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2076482#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2076226" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2076226" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Tagimaucia"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1173775"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1173775.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Tagimaucia" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Addict-Eau-Fraiche-2014-25611.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.25611.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Dior Addict Eau Fraiche 2014"title="Dior Addict Eau Fraiche 2014"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2076226ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2076226" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1173775">Tagimaucia</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-27">02/27/24 18:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Can iris be sexy? YES SIR!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2076226"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2076226#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2075050" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2075050" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="NOSEYBODY"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1259603"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1259603.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="NOSEYBODY" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2075050ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2075050" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1259603">NOSEYBODY</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-26">02/26/24 15:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Dior Homme Parfum opens with the usual "Lipstick" Iris note. Also within that opening you get a note of Italian Orange. <br />
<br />
Its not a bright zesty sweet Orange. Its immediately heavy, soured, &amp; somewhat Boozy, like Grand Marnier. <br />
<br />
For reference, It smells like the Booze in Fahrenheit Le Parfum mixed with a Sour Orange note.<br />
<br />
The Rose is beautifully supported by the note of Sandalwood. But its not a natural Rose. Its Cosmetic. Like a Rose scented Makeup Powder.<br />
<br />
Within the initial opening theres also the heavy presence of a Green, almost minty cool, yet warm Spice swirling around that smells like an unlisted note of Cardamom.<br />
<br />
Just as soon as Dior Homme Parfum begins to settle into this Spiced Rose scented Makeup Powder with Boozy Orange undertones, in comes this note of Leather, which not only darkens the fragrance, but also causes it to straddle the fence in ambiguity.<br />
<br />
To my nose the Leather is roughed up. More like Nubuck than smooth Leather. However its not strong. Its moderate &amp; blended well within the other notes.<br />
<br />
All of this rests on a bed of Agarwood, Cedar, &amp; Ambrette. <br />
<br />
The Agarwood note is not the "Oud" variety we've come to expect. This Agarwood is Woody, Soft, Dusty, &amp; acts as a base for the Cedar note. <br />
<br />
The note of Ambrette in this fragrance isnt exactly Musky in the way you'd think. It smells warm, &amp; mildly ambry sweet, like dark human skin.<br />
<br />
To be perfectly honest, Dior Homme Parfum smells like a Middle Eastern interpretation of Dior Homme. <br />
<br />
In fact, in the Night Air Dior Homme Parfum smells like a Luxury Rose Incense you'd smell burned in Middle Eastern Palaces during Wedding Parties. <br />
<br />
The fragrance isnt Smoky. But the Dustiness of the Agarwood creates the feeling of Incense.<br />
<br />
The combination of Ambrette, Soured Orange, &amp; Cardamom also creates an accord that tricks my nose into smelling Myrrh somewhere in the composition.<br />
<br />
The final dry down of DHP is a leathery, dusty vanilla-like, ambry sweet Rose/Agarwood skin scent with spices. <br />
<br />
In this stage the Spice/Rose combination smells very similar to the Spice/Rose combination in Dior's "Oud Ispahan", but without the Oud, &amp; Cowhide Leather accord..<br />
<br />
Unlike other reviewers I will not say that if you like Dior Homme Intense you'll like Dior Homme Parfum. Because they're two entirely different fragrances. <br />
<br />
However, I will say that even though Dior Homme Parfum has accords of both Lipstick &amp; Makeup Powder, &amp; straddles the fence in ambiguity, that just like Dior Homme Intense, it still leans more Masculine than it does Feminine. <br />
<br />
The performance of Dior Homme Parfum is through the roof. Its strong, but its so pleasant that its not intrusive. <br />
<br />
For anyone experiencing performance issues with a newly sprayed bottle. Let it macerate for two weeks to a month after its initial few sprays. You will see an improvement in its performance, as well as more depth to its scent.<br />
<br />
Its a dark fragrance, but its not brooding. Its more of a mysterious darkness. Quite different from Dior Homme Intense, which is more of a sexy darkness.<br />
<br />
Dior Homme Parfum is among my most complimented fragrances. So have no worries there. <br />
<br />
Dior Homme Parfum is the most complex fragrance in the Dior Homme Line. Its a true masterpiece, &amp; a must have for fragrance collectors, if you can still find it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2075050"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2075050#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2073907" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2073907" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="iRankFragrances"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1959678"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1959678.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="iRankFragrances" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Lorenzo-Pazzaglia/Summer-Hammer-81476.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.81476.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Summer Hammer"title="Summer Hammer"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2073907ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2073907" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1959678">iRankFragrances</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-25">02/25/24 14:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is top tier. I recently got this fragrance and so far I have gotten many compliments of it. It is really strong on the iris and surprisingly orange has a strong smell aswell. It's so addictive and smells like a powerful orange soda mixed with the most deep iris ever and then blends in with the leather drydown.<br />
<br />
It smells like a rich man who owns a huge car collection.<br />

I have bashed DHI for the lip stick woman’s make up bag thing for a while now. I generally refuse to jump on any hype train and follow a crowd, which is why my collection consists mainly of niche and indie houses. BUT THIS DHP is different. I never planned to try it bc I thought it would just be an amped up version of DHI. Well, I finally got me a decant. A gentleman was nice enough to send it as a surprise with my recent purchase of PDM - Oajan…<br />
 <br />
DHP is pure class and sophistication. It smells much more expensive than what it really is. It is one of the sexiest leather fragrances I’ve ever smelled. It is not like DHI with the lipstick make up bag at all, it’s there but not in your face like that one. This is a really really good take on leather. It’s not like a leather wallet or belt type of leather, it’s like a new high end French leather couch where someone who was wearing DHI was sitting on it next to a bad bitch. It lasted on my hand all day and through the night. I couldn’t stop smelling it and it just kept getting better on my skin, more creamy and seductive, prob from the sandalwood. <br />
<br />
I see why people love this one so much. I will never purchase DHI or any other flanker from the line, but I have just ordered DHP w the F U tax to America. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1544521">0xrafae</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-22">02/22/24 12:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Dior Homme has been my go-to for formal nights out, but Homme Parfum just takes that excellence to another level. The shift from Intense is subtle, but the addition of a gentle orange note makes a stunning difference. It's going to be quite some time before anyone can follow Demachy and outdo his previous nearly flawless creation.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2070628"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2070628#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2065620" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2065620" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Carlitos"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1071323"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1071323.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Carlitos" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Elixir-68415.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.68415.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Sauvage Elixir"title="Sauvage Elixir"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2065620ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2065620" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1071323">Carlitos</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-17">02/17/24 17:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>"OUI" FOR A 2011 DIOR... BUT PARFUM OR INTENSE?<br />
[short review]<br />
<br />
The Dior Homme series is sometimes hated and often loved. Perhaps it is the most consensual male perfume of the elite trio Chanel-Dior-YSL. Of course, I am not referring to any of the perfume versions that have been launched in 2020. I am writing about the good old 2011 versions that you can still encounter in many WEB retailers.<br />
These Dior stars - as well its Valentino satellites and its Zara and Armaf's asteroids - have in common a noticeable Iris note. Then the different perfume offers may grant you a little more or a little less vanilla, ambrette, cedar, or even leather and cocoa. Performance and quality are proportional to the above-average price.<br />
Usually, the most serious perfume aficionados prefer Homme Parfum 2011 or Homme Intense 2011 within the Dior offer.<br />
Dior Homme Parfum and Valentino Uomo EDT are the fragrances that stray furthest from this strong Iris note backbone. The Dior Parfum version has a musky footprint due to the Ambrette note and, of all the perfumes mentioned so far, it is the only one that has a faint Oud note added to Sandalwood.<br />
I am not a strong fan of Iris so I may have some distance and fairness to compare these various fragrances, even if coming from different brands. On the other hand, I love Oud but I was never completely convinced that there is real harmony in a blending of Oud and Iris.<br />
I do like Dior Homme Parfum but I confess that as a spraying choice on my skin is punctual for me. I do it only when I find myself looking for a darker mood or when the weather is very cold. Most of the time I prefer the more wearable Intense version ... and I also never let anybody take away from me my beloved and sweeter Valentino Uomo EDT for brighter and warmer days. But if it's really cold, the Dior Homme Parfum thicker scent becomes irresistible, besides giving us the best performance with enviable longevity, sillage and projection.<br />
Dior Homme Parfum is mostly a linear fragrance and, right from the start, shows you an earthy and powdery Iris. You perceive a growing velvety manly leather that will become dominant for a couple of hours and will faint during the drydown. A soft oriental but dark sandalwood, as well a musky background, are easily detectable. Together they will take over for the drydown.<br />
It's a sunset and sunrise type of fragrance.<br />
<br />
Music: Pink Floyd - "Dark Side of The Moon"</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2065620"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2065620#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2063858" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Good for formal occasions.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2057407"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2057407#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2057022" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2057022" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ChiliOfTheValley"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1629944"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1629944.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ChiliOfTheValley" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Marc-Antoine-Barrois/Ganymede-54720.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.54720.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Ganymede"title="Ganymede"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2057022ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2057022" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1629944">ChiliOfTheValley</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-09">02/09/24 05:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Not being satisfied with the performance of DHI, I pulled the trigger on this expecting it to be DHI on steroids, with beastly performance on par with Sauvage Elixir. Sounds good, right? Hell nah. This couldn’t be further from the truth. I am so disappointed.<br />
<br />
All the reviewers here saying “use no more than 2 sprays, or you might choke out the nearest person”, “impossible to wear in closed spaces” must be smelling a different fragrance or older batches. Seems like DHP has been reformulated to death.<br />
<br />
I have a 2023 batch, and the scent is simply gorgeous, really refined. It definitely has that “wow!” factor and it smells so much better than DHI, which is already a beauty on its own. But hear me out, even with 3-4 sprays, I guarantee people won’t be able to smell you. This is a very intimate fragrance. The most I could get out of this is about 2 hours soft projection and 7-8 hours longevity with a minimum of 4 sprays.<br />
<br />
I’m pretty sure older batches perform much better, this fragrance has a solid rating for a reason. But if you’re looking to pick up a recent batch, consider that the performance of newer batches is mediocre (at best) before buying.<br />
<br />
TL;DR: You’re paying 150 euros for a skin scent. I think the price here is definitely not justified.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2057022"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2057022#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2056800" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1317182">Blizznakov</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-27">01/27/24 11:36</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a tough one to describe. One thing is for sure, this is the best one from the Dior Homme line. It took me a whole year to get a bottle of DHP (Dior Homme Parfum) and i have mixed feeling about it. On the good side, like i said this is the best version of Dior Homme, also it has the best performance, the sprayer is perfect like any other dior, the scent is 100% complete, super unique and sophisticated. Now on the down side, it's hard to get, just because it's unique doesn't mean that you will like it, you can't imagine the scent from notes, the juice is niche quality, but lacks some flashy presentation like most niche fragrances, it just comes in a rectangular, carton dior box.<br />
However the scent is i soo well blended. Imagine a mix of leather, light sweet smoke and sweet iris. It feels like it has a pinch of chocolate/cacao although it is not mentioned in the notes. The longevity is easily 9-10 hours and projecting pretty well for 3-6 hours. I don't know why, but on my skin the scent is not consistent. Sometime i go noseblind to it really fast and some times i can feel it more or later after few hours. It's weird. Anyway i admire DHP and appreciate it even though i'm not in love with it. This fragrance is like a excellent and expensive smoking suit, you know it's the best looking official dress you got, but you can't wear it all the time.<br />
<br />
Bottle Design: 7.5<br />
Longevity: 7.5<br />
Projection Power: 7<br />
Projection Time: 6<br />
Scent: 8<br />
Price: 7<br />
Overall: 7.16<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2037505" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="NoirMemoir"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1329296"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1329296.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="NoirMemoir" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Creed/Silver-Mountain-Water-472.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.472.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Silver Mountain Water"title="Silver Mountain Water"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2037505ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2037505" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1329296">NoirMemoir</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-21">01/21/24 10:03</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After getting a sample of Dior Homme Intense a while ago, and also a sample of Mancera Black Prestigium, i was really eager to test the now legendary Dior Homme Parfum. I wanted it to be the same experience as with Layton vs Layton Exclusif where the original was nice but Exclusif was "WOW!". I wanted Dior Homme Parfum to bring the "dirtyness" and the matureness.<br />
<br />
Bought a small decant of DHP from someone and now im seriously suspecting i might have been scammed and whats in the vial is actually the normal DHI.  <br />
<br />
From the decant i've got, i smell no leather, no oud, just the lipstick iris with a strong rose. As im writing this, i sprayed both the older DHI sample and DHP decant on my hands and i smell no difference.<br />
<br />
I brought up Mancera's Black Prestigium because i think, in a way, it "clones" Dior Homme Intense but what it does is it cranks up the rose accord way too much, and its the signature Montale rose. I don't hate the rose used often in Montale/Mancera, but i think its a bit overdosed in Black Prestigium just for the sake of adding their own signature to it. The rose in Mancera makes it more synthetic, unpolished while Dior focuses on the powdery Iris and is a bit sweeter and velvety. Dior is smooth all together, while Black Prestigium is wild and screetchy for a good couple of hours but alot better as the hours go by and i even prefer the late drydown of it to Dior's.<br />
<br />
Im bummed out because eighter i got scammed and Dior Homme Parfum eluded me, or my nose just cannot make a difference from Dior Homme Intense and frankly i don't know which of the two is worst haha.<br />
<br />
Final update: With my last drops of DHI i made one more side by side comparition to Parfum and i was wrong because there is a difference. Parfum dials down the sweetness and adds the rose note which makes it more synthetic, more feminine and less appealing to me. People who get intrigued by the Parfum version haven't dabbled much in Middle Eastern perfumery.  <br />
<br />
I pick DHI over all 3 fragrances not only because its cheaper, but it simply is more versatile and smells better.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2037505"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2037505#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2036973" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1753657">Felixthreeone</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-18">01/18/24 19:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is, quite simply, magnificent. The quality of perfumery contained inside of this bottle is exquisite. I just finally got my nose on a decant and all I can say is wow. The way this unfolds is every bit of what the note breakdown suggests, but in a way that the notes themselves simply cannot convey. You must smell this if you are even remotely a fan of the Dior line of iris-based fragrances. Or even if you aren't. If you like fragrance, you need to smell this. And wear it. It isn't a blind-buy safe fragrance, although if you like DHI, VUI, rose, leather and oud this is right up your alley. I do admit that it is a bit less dry than I thought it would be, and the rose is a bit more pronounced than I was expecting. That aside, I'm not sure this fragrance is something I want to own a bottle of. I'm not sure when I could deploy such a beautiful fragrance into the world. Even the most posh, sophisticated event that I will ever attend in my life isn't proper enough for this level of fragrant perfection. The parfum would be wearing me the whole time. If you can pull this off, my hat is off to you sir/ma'am. This is the pinnacle of designer Dior, in my honest opinion. I'm sure some of the OG Homme mixes were stellar, but this is the only one I've been fortunate enough to experience. Sample this, if you can. You may be blown away, as I was. Or, you may not. But, you may be that person that can wear this with regularity and that is great too.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2035146"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2035146#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2033420" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2017525" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="MrDanish"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1473678"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1473678.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="MrDanish" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-de-Parfum-48100.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.48100.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Sauvage Eau de Parfum"title="Sauvage Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2017525ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2017525" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1473678">MrDanish</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-02">01/02/24 01:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If you're a man of the cloth in southern Europe or fancy yourself smelling like the occult lair below the church floor, this is for you.<br />
<br />
For everybody else, realize that it's borderline discontinued for a reason and that you will most likely find Dior Homme Intense much more appealing, even if you dislike iris.<br />
<br />
This one is dry, damp, musky, incency and not at all sweet. Pretty much as it says on the tin, but don't think that this is a floral scent or something welcoming, because it's not. It's a leather bound, antique book smashed directly in your face, which insists on staying as a curse, once it's touched your skin and clothes.<br />
<br />
If you're still aiming for something dramatic from the house of Dior, Sauvage Elixir is a much better bet. <br />
<br />
P.S. as an afterthought, I think you might like it as an accessory if you're into outdoor fantasy role play, but spray lightly or they will pick up your scent trail. The light spray is also recommended if you're into S/M, given that you're the master, or your slave might choke completely ;)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2017525"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2017525#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2017122" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2013155" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Bababrr"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1695936"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1695936.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Bababrr" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Nishane/Hacivat-44174.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.44174.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Hacivat"title="Hacivat"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2013155ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2013155" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1695936">Bababrr</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-28">12/28/23 09:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My favourite fragrance of all time. <br />
<br />
The most elegant, luxurious and addictive scent I have. Very high quality ingredients used, that work magically with each other. The iris is still the main player and is just as lipsticky as in DHI, but is backed up with such smooth leather and woodsy qualities. In the complete dry down after about 7-8 hours, I get subtle and sweet rose and it’s my favourite part. Such a comforting scent. You feel special when you wear this and you will until that day is done. <br />
<br />
Longevity is exceptional, with 12+ hours of strong projecting and radiating goodness. Lasts as a skin scent until the next day but I don’t count that, as it already has beyond enough lasting power for a whole day. <br />
<br />
Definitely suited for evening and night time use in the Autumn and Winter. Best for special occasions and special moments but this would be the best signature scent, if bottles of this was far more widely available. <br />
<br />
I was lucky enough to be able to get the last remaining bottle at a duty free in an airport for an amazing price back in September and I’ve held off on reviewing this to give it time. This being a blind buy, and me not being that big of a fan of DHI, this truly took me by my feet.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="2013155"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=2013155#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="27417" sentiment="all"></reviews-infinity>

<br />
<br />
Oh, here it is! The long-awaited Parfum derivative of Dior Homme is finally in the database! And I have to say 'wow'. This is certainly a stunning release from the Maison of Christian Dior. <br />
<br />
I discovered the Parfum a week ago while wandering around in Boulevard Haussman's Lafayette, looking for l'Orpheline by Serge Lutens (check it out, it's great), when something on the Dior shelf caught my eye.. I was like: a new flanker? Nah, it can't be. I asked for further information and the saleswoman confirmed it to me: it was indeed an avant-première of the latest Dior Homme release. Such a great surprise... I looked up on Fragrantica: no trace of it. So I'll try to give you a quick recap of my first impressions after 2 days of wearing and testing:<br />
<br />
DHP gives us a magistral opening with the famous signature tuscan iris. The DH identity is still very strong during the first minutes, with a gourmandish feel similar to DHI, but with more woods. That opus doesn't last long though: the Parfum rapidly morphs into a dark and opulent woody scent, with a heavy and rich sandalwood -  oudwood(?) accord, sitting on a dry, smoky, upper class/niche style leather. <br />
<br />
I can also detect a lot of incense, that, along with the smoky/powdery leather and the oudwood/sandalwood accord, gives the Parfum an oriental and a lightly medicinal vibe, which is very pleasant: noble without being too 'dirty'. Furthermore, the Dior saleswoman talked about a rose note in the parfum. I tried to make it out, with little success.<br />
<br />
Compared to DHI (which is the first fragrance somebody is naturally going to compare the parfum with), the Parfum is dryer, with almost no vanilla, a toned down iris/makeup-ish note and an accentuated woody-leathery side. It also smells more oriental than gourmand, if it makes any sense. In any way, this is *not* a more potent version of DHI. This could almost be a whole new fragrance, or actually be part of the Collection Privée, really. <br />
<br />
DHP has its own character and really makes a statement: <br />
<br />
☞ woody (prominent sweet sandalwood - oudwood accord) <br />
☞ leathery (dry, sour and smoky)<br />
☞ oriental (incense, more incense, and medicinal oudwood)<br />
☞ slightly animalic (musk, DH style ambrette)<br />
☞ powdery (DH DNA with the tuscan iris)<br />
<br />
<br />
Longevity is truly amazing: 20 hours on my skin with three sprays (two in the neck, one on the wrist), shower included. When it comes to sillage, it is surprisingly not that heavy, although it can easily fill a room during the first hour. I found the Parfum to be easier to wear and versatile than the EdP (DHI), and just like DH and DHI, DHP could without a doubt be a unisex scent. <br />
<br />
I also got complimented a couple of times (yes, already). The bottle design is similar to DHI's bottle. It feels very heavy, with a darker design, and a huge black collar at the top of the glass part. The juice has an intensely ambery color: it leaves a very clear light brown stain on white clothes.<br />
<br />
<br />
To conclude, it seems that Dior is striking again, with superior quality blending and ingredients, pushing the Dior Homme line to a whole new level. This parfum screams pure luxury and is absolutely worth all the hype. Even the niche competition will have a hard time beating such a high quality composition... <br />
Could this be a sort of new, Dior-style M7 with iris?... I'm wondering.<br />
<br />
<br />
The star of my next winter! ✓<br />
<br />
<br />
Ps. with all due respect to Dior's ambassador, I don't think Robert Pattison advertises the Parfum very well... it is definitely not a "young and casual" scent. I rather see a gentleman in his 40s-50s in a tuxedo, enjoying a good whiskey and a cigar in a hotel jazz club at night wearing this (Bill Murray in Lost in Translation maybe?).<br />
<br />
_</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="513511"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=513511#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1804839" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/661994">edge42</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2014-12-24">12/24/14 09:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Francois Demachy turns to the "dark side"!<br />
<br />
If Dior Homme is Luke Skywalker, then Dior Homme Intense is Princess Leia. That makes Dior Homme Parfum Darth Vader, the true badass of the family. The dark, loud and unapologetic one. But also the one everyone treats with the most respect. <br />
<br />
Imagine a richer, darker, more daring and incredibly strong version of Dior Homme and you'll be pretty close. Rose has definitely shown up to this Dior party, and it's dressed up as Darth Vader in a leather jacket. Leather and rose are very prominent throughout the scent, especially the drydown. And both are very beautiful notes that are extremely well done.<br />
<br />
And what a powerhouse! This stuff is crazy, probably the most powerful fragrance I've ever come across. The juice is very yellow/brown with an obviously high concentration of perfume oil (so be careful what you spray it on!). High quality oil as is the Dior way. Seriously, 1 spray of this has lasted over 1 week (!!!) on a sample cotton pad, and it's still projecting over 1 foot. This scent goes through about 4-5 different distinct stages over the course of DAYS. Not hours, the scent lasts so long that some of the later drydown stages don't show up for a day or two... I don't even know what else to say!<br />
<br />
Ha, I don't think I've ever written a review with so many exclamation marks before. If you love Dior Homme, this is a definite try. But you'd better be prepared to come to the dark side.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="552055"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=552055#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1723209" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1194785">Le Chypriote</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-05-24">05/24/19 13:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>WARNING: Do not blind buy this fragrance!<br />
<br />
'Beast Mode' is an understatement when describing the projection power of this perfume. This flanker is an absolute nuclear iris bomb that explodes with a powerful, assertive, yet sensual aroma. Anyone caught within the "blast zone" will feel its radiant iris and powdery "fallout".<br />
<br />
The evolution of this scent is very long; the iris dominates for a good 24 hours, with leather and sandalwood in the back.<br />
<br />
It took me two showers to scrub the scent off, and even then I could still smell the faintest "half life" of this fragrance on my skin.<br />
<br />
I can appreciate what Dior has done with this flanker, but am unable to wear such scents due to the sheer intensity of their aroma. <br />
<br />
Use no more than 2 sprays, or you might choke out the nearest person.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="27417"comment_id="1063696"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html?ccid=1063696#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent977885" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc977885" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TrephineArtist"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1135869"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1135869.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TrephineArtist" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Al-Haramain-Perfumes/Max-d-19814.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.19814.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Max'd"title="Max'd"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma977885ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd977885" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1135869">TrephineArtist</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-09-02">09/02/18 06:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Finally I got around to trying this and wow this is not for me!<br />
<br />
It smells of an old musky leather &amp; fur (ie rotting skin) handbag with remnants of vintage make-up and dust. I'm puzzled as to why any man (in particular) would want to smell like this but that's the beauty of fragrance and individual tastes I suppose, we're all different.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/800105">khosro.zk</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2014-12-23">12/23/14 05:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Gorgeous smell. Excellent performance. The only huge difference between this fragrance and Dior Homme Intense (DHI) is the leather scent that exists here. The leather here introduced a type of bitter smell to it that is not my favorite. Maybe this scent made it more mature or more masculine, but I prefer the DHI over the perfume version. It is somehow more fresh and sweet.  <br />
